youre vertue dothe defend iniurye hande making ye maiſtrys hart craue cōſent lawfull mariage ſocietio wedlocke whereby thaunciente mutynies ciuill grudge ſhall onlye retire receaue ende howſes reioyned eftſones indiſſoluble bonde affynitye betwene v ſhal lyue hereafter contynuall quiet enioyenge mutuall amytie firme ſtronge partes former quarrells fatal ful mortalytie theſe newes ſtayinge courſe wonted teares diſmiſſinge withal al dollorous argumentes regardes ſorowe ſturred vppe ſuche complexion dye natural white redde face faire syennoyse ſhe ſeamed rather goddes ſyttinge gliſtering troane ymppe creature nature forcinge ſuche vehemencye deſyer harte salymbyno dryuen efteſones geue ſecōd charg goodwil franke offer make participation vnto halfe liuinge richeſſe wherewyth ſhee preſented hym ſemelye reuerence maieſtye modeſtie womanly behauiour retorninge requeſt thanks due liberal offer aſſurance part omit neyther indeuor diligence declaration dutie behalfe hym god hathe reſerued laweful huſbande companion bedde wherewith ſpent ſome litle momente embraſinge one certein kyſſes giuen receiued recyprocallye betwene theim anseamo knocked olde awnte lyenge houſe whoſe charge fydelytie commytted glorie newe conqueſte fyndinge leaſte momente delaye greatly hurteful deſyer diſpatched ymediatlye ſeueral meſſengers deare neareſt parentes frendes obeyinge expedition ſhort ſommance came ymediatelye vnto houſe requeſted aſſiſtance aduiſe companye conſommacion buſynes greate importance wherein appered willinge liked requeſt ſeamed ſewer vſe aboue ordinarie ſeleritie thexecuiion enterpriſe ſending awnte new charge deare angeliqva repaired immediatly oute greate amaze frendes pallaies montanin ſkarcely giuinge leaue interteynementes proffer court wherwith charles ſaluted hym companye recited hys newe brother lawe hearinge reſt longe ſince ſyſter came lodginge requeſt communicate ſecrete ſo parte hee nowe afore hym reueale ſuche thinges hadd determined ſince departure publike audience witnes companie whiche hadd aſſembled purpoſe al worlde intended imparte rare honeſtie vertue ſuche reuenge himſelfe mente take vppon theim ſeamed honoure offer pleaſure ſurmounte gifte thank efull dealyng whiche wordes ſeamed ende whole companye ſet order erſpectacion ſée theffecte miſterie beinge ſcilence torned face oraciō multitude theſe tearmes thinkes ſée wonderfull amaze ſeuerall ymaginacion entente procuringe aſſemblie salymbyn frendes ſo mariage angeliqua ſo inconueniente hower ſuche place none kinſmen frends ſelfe hetherunto haue euer ſett foote enter without deſier endomage ſome notable harme reſte theym remaine montanyn lyne whiche aſtoniſhement ſhall alſo ſuſpende till ende ſhorte preamble haue preferred better vnderſtā dinge parte meane playe conſider regarde indifferent iudgement waighe equal ballance thinge whiche called good harte ſuche differrynge brutall ſorte followe parte raiſon properly called ſpiritual ſhall ſee meane generoſytie highe harte grafted v greate myſtres firſte mother dame nature doth neuer ceaſe make ſhewe ſeuerall effectes ſometyme bringinge furthe one vertue ſometime makynge declaration whiche alſo preferre theyr ſondrye frutes accordynge excellencie noble ſprynge fyrſte ſource ſame wherein alſo nobylitie minde hath ſuche force ſpeciall priuiledge fyrſte founder albeit humaine thinges framed vertue firme ſubiect chāge mettall inſtabilitye ſubiecte chaunge yet ſhe founde firme voide reuolucion thoughe ſhe bée one chiefe marke whereat dame fortune doth loaſe inconſtante arrowes ſhakynge perſynge dartes againſte ſydes yet ſhee founde ſoo inuincible noble mynde inuincible agaynſt fortune againſte aſſaultes ſhee voyde power moue bluſtrynge windes forcynge incredible furye angrye diſpoſition ſea ſeame vnhable ſturre harde rocke ſtonye montayne vppon followeth greatnes fortune wyth glee infynite rich doo lifte vppe make ſwell harte villaine one baſe condicion ſyniſter chaunge eſtate anye malyce miniſters pouertye embaſe make ſtowpe greatenes corage theym wroughte contrary frame made ſtuffe vulgare ſorte kepe alwayes maieſtie theyr originall obſerue ſuche ſorte thinſtincte bloode whereof theyr aunceſtors made noble gaue theym ſucke veray milke vertue diſpites malicious ſomonce ſoeuer fortune doth ſende theim temperat argument modeſtie complexion countenaunce wyth true effect operation true vertue mind ſufficientlye argue condicion defyinge threates worlde make abſolute declaration vnder vaile ſuche miſerie ſhrowded harte deſeruinge better allowance aduerſatie whiche tormentes theym herein conſiſtes whole glorye youthe persian king cyrunoriſhed brought vp contreye meade albeit noriſhed broughte vppe amongeſte heardmenne parentes yet gaue place contrey magnanymytie mynde hath exceded bene equall generoſytie noble corage harte romvlvs firſte founder prowde romulus brought vp amonge ſhepherdes cytie rome yet hée aſſiſted better educacion trayninge vppe thenne caues cabynettes ſhepherdes ſuche inhabyte playne deſerte fieldes garde cattell whyche haue preferred vnto lord ladyes ſpecial prepratiue peculiar praiſe commendacion vndowted noblenes mynde signevr charles montanyn ſyſter wythoute preiudice wronge anye maye well tearmed peragon bewtie mirroer honeſte chaſte behauioure aboue lady annd gentlewoman oure common wealthe whoſe houſe knowe hathe bene ſo oppreſſed wythe contynual perſecucion onely two laſte remeyndoures whole race ſtandinge alſo longe ſince pointe extreme ruyne vtter ſubuerſion euer yet ympociſion ſuche ſtraunge crueltie aunceſtors reſpecte ſmal broyle happeninge chaunce hathe moued thonder moſt mortal vengance ſo auncient vertuous ſtocke part pryuie mine vnlavvfull vvinning father cō me iuſt loſſe ſonne conſcience remembrance wiſe admonicion graue philoſopher ſaying vnlawfull winninge father come iuſte loſſe ſonne ſoo hee make himſelfe tyrante force becomes oftentimes ſlaue iuſtice thinke neceſſarye onelye blowe laſte retraite grudge betwene v alſo worke effecte confirmation future amytie euer hereafter view thauncient quarrel mutunies former time ſtaye conſente preſent compaſſion caſe yet let honeſt trade lyfe ciuill behauiour modeſt diſpoſition brother ſyſter depart without due mede hyer vertue neyther let v ſuffer place ſenate bee emptie voyde ſupplie earſte hathe bene furniſhed preſence indeuours nowe becauſe ſée alredie ſorowearyed lengthe lingrynge ſuſpence deſyerynge knowe cauſe thys greate commendaciou montanyns requeſt abridge tediouſe diſcourſe lende yet litle liberty ſpeake patience heare chiefe poyntes proteſtation ſpedie ende tale ſhal reſtore preſent quiet contentment trobled myndes longe ſince muſte confeſſe yet thoffence neyther mortal falte ſo hainous may forgiuen beauty part perfection faire angeliqua preſente ſo rauiſhed ſences robbed libertie one inſtant thonly exerciſe whych occupyed head daye nighte longe tyme ſondrye deuiſes ymagyned diſcouer vnto martiredome wherin fedd hongry humor affection ſuch alarams contraryetie conceites hauinge thys meane loſte neceſſary appetite ſtomake vſual deſyer ſleepe felte ſuche diminucion nature lyuelye force thorowe partes preſented one tyme wyth choice two moſte perillous euils worlde one dye afore tyme ſuffocacion pynnynge dollour el yelde depriuation ſences gyfte vnderſtandinge euer wherein alſo purſued wyth readye aſſiſtaunce perplexed diſpaire ſaw meane make ſeame eaſye wherein iudged ſo greate impoſſibilitye chieflye grounded quarels oure ij houſes whereby albeit warre ſeames ended grudge halfe appaiſed betwene v yet opinyon remeined equall deſyer harte v neyther wiſhe well one muche leſſe abſteine ſlaughter ſo euer newe occaſion ſhoulde efteſones fall oute neyther coulde theis mortall impedimentes argue ſufficient raiſon diminiſh min affection ſturred vp rather treble increaſe deſyer accordynge paſſioned minde enchaunted loue make ſuche poſſeſſeth apte deſyre loue make v apte deſier hable attaine hable attayne effect whiche wiſhe preferrynge alwayes ſimple likelihode wherin appereth abſolute impoſſibilitye thende afflicte theyr miſerable lyues wyth continuall annoye theis extremeties filled head full diſpaire committed continuall carefulnes minde becauſe coulde neither ſtaye courſe affection encounter obiect deſyer beholde fortune entred compaſſion ſtate aſſiſtynge wyth ſo readye medecine greate diſeaſe voyde expectation hope recouerye preſented franke offer deſyered praye vnknowen ſence departure viij ten dayes lord montanyn preſent beinge accuſed afore senate vppon certeine peinall ſtatutes deuiſed cruell ſtate rappeale baniſhed men awarded iudiciall ſentence paye forfaiture whiche becauſe coulde ont nottender within tyme greadie enemy forced ye law rigour neceſſarie ſuche ſort thexecutioner readie extende vpon bodie want ſupplye thoſande florents choake couetous humour magiſtrates euen ſo view extremitie ſturred vp ſuch remorce mynde thought ſommoned dutie preuent deſtruction brother thonly comfort alredye proclaimed ſoueraigne ladye myſtres hart whiche good vaine deuocion payd money procured delyuerye parte deuinynge tell vpon occaſion beautie ſiſter worke theffect ſuche vertue hath onely thankefull benefit alſo ouercome honeſte liberalitie true noblenes mynde preſenting beginnynge eueninge myne owne howſe prodigal offer onely hymſelf al yt hath alſo ſyſter lefte vſe diſpoſe pleaſure wherein ende appeale one requeſte waighinge rightly gyfte one offer conſider aſſiſte immediatly wyth aduiſe ſorte maye yelde due meede ſuche ij precious merites one moſt familiar patterne precedent true nobilitie preſent ſuche price value greateſt prince italy coulde wronge greatnes yeldynge honor homage ſo rare thing wherupon ſtayed diſcourſe gyuinge place thaſſiſtantes conſultacion caſe whiche albeit knewe imported deliberat aduiſe afore reſolution iudgement yet amaze ſentence gyue becauſe neither priuie partaker determinacion hym ſommoned apparance rather witnes fact deuide caſe impeſhe reſolute intent contrarye councell lady kynſwomen ſo moued admiracion wyth maieſtie argumentes vertue faire angeliqva paſſed iudgement ſyde yf feared refuſed hym wiſhed voice waye onely beinge touched aboue reſt moſt neare quicke diſmiſſed aſtoniſhment reueilyng owne determination ſorte seinge take ſo greate tyme diſcuſſe ſo ſmall matter leſſe angeliqva hande hauynge regarde honor afore myne eye deſyer recompenſe full honeſtye vertue brother reſolued take ſyſter deare lawfull wyfe preferrynge meanes perfect vnitye whiche longe tyme hath lyued ſeparacion make twoo bodyes earſte longe diſioyned equall wyll entyer mynde deſyerynge conſentes conſommation alliance whiche ſeameth rather worke god effect councell diligence man lawe mariage mariage firſt thing vvherin chriſt glorified himſelf miracle beynge inſtitution higheſt thinge wherin chriſt firſt glorified himſelf miracle vpon earth recorded thinfallible booke foreknowledge thende nothynge chaunce whiche permitted forſeene prouidence god marueils ſewerlye layed hande vpon brother montanyn touching diſtreſſe perill lyfe thende angeliqva onely meane thy delyuerye might alſo laye immouable fondacion mutuall vnitie betwene two houſes hope ſhall furuiue length tyme ende wyth laſte remeinder eyther poſterityes concluſion thus hearde parentes kynſfolkes salymbyno canuaiſed alitle ſeuerall opinion ſeamed laſte ſuche reaſon indifferencie conuerted conceites whiche kepte occupyed tyme preſent diſpoſition wonderfull ioye gladnes feelynge theyr intrals inwarde partes tell ſecret inſtinct minde approche indiſſoluble tranquillitie partes coniunction newe allyance albeit equalitye porciō ye dowere angeliqva ſtoode aloff reuenues newe conſort yet vertue giftes grace appearyng made ſeame hable counteruaile hym reſpect frendes one voice gaue generall commendacion goodnes fortune plātyng affection ſo vertuous ſoyle wherein ſewerly good reaſon mariage law holye sacrament giuen v god thonly knott mutuall tranquillitie betwene man choice vvife vvee ought reſpect vertue gyftes mind rich exterior beautye woman oughte embraſed vertue ſinceritie thynge abuſed regarde richeſſe fylthye promocious worlde choice wyfe reſpectes chieflye beautie greatnes porcion beſides thouſand pettie mutynies fall houſekeping eſcapeth ſeldom without ſprit grudge cyuill diſcenſion diſturbynge hys quiet wyth continuall humour frettynge diſpoſition féedynge hys mynde glaſſe beautie retireth gyueth place age whiche alſo mortifyeth delite deſyer pleaſure thother ſyde woman knowynge diſcent noble porcion excede welthe huſbande forgetteth take hart graſſe deckynge garlande wyth ſortes flower pryde diſdayne ſéekes gouerne gett vpper hande hym appointed heade woordes ſcripture inſtitution nature oughte kepe ſtraite hande ſame bridle raine authoritie vſinge chek reſtraine deſyer libertie ſtudieth haue hym ſubiection wherein wiſhe bachilors younge men vnmaried armed againſte ſo greate miſchiefe experience ſuche theyr frendes ſee touched like griefe part lament diſquiet woulde rather dare attempte ſimple reformacion borne beare yoke awe commandement huſbandes retournynge therewyth ſequeile salymbyno workynge laſte effect conſommation curteſye gaue one halfe goodes ſortes fauour mariage adopting thinſtant montanyn brother lawe aſſured frende generall ſubſtitution goodes chaunced dye without heire bodye hauyng child conueighed vnto hym ſuche aſſuraunce reuercion lawe coulde deuiſe moytie whiche gaue dowerye faire angeliqva whome sonday folowynge maried pompe due eſtates vniuerſall contentement frendes ſpeciall quiet citye endured longe affliction mortalitie ciuill warre theis ij houſes suche variety happenyng ſucceſſe wordly affaire wherein wil denye aduerſitie ſomtime neceſſarie men ſeinge ſhe doth force wonderfull remorce reformacion lyfe aduerſitie neceſſary make v parfect alſo workes often tymes effect wherin appeared abſolute impoſſibilitie conqueſt meane truly vertue example diſcredites vtterly commendacion auncient romaine amongeſte whome chaunced diuerſe tymes greate enimyties grudge mynde ſo folowed ſpedie reconcilement albeit ſuche meanes franke attonement betwene salymbyns montanyns ſome reclaymed offer promocion ſome ſolicited voice whole common welth confirmed preſent gyfte ſome notable office regard peculyar proffit one approchynge neare magnanimitie worſte theſe three whereof one ſommoned paſſion loue ſcamed excede nature perfourmynge exploit hable anye waye el wrought effect yet cryenge againſte loue paintes hym cullors rage follye frenzye ſuche rather abuſed wyth theyr owne conceites hable conſider ryghtelye vertue impreſſion loue noble harte thing true ſubiecte curteſye fountaine whence diſtilleth originall cyuill good order vertues loue noble minde onelye meane moue v moderacion inclined crueltie reuenge chiefeſt norſſe preſeruer peace amongeſt men wherein yf ſome vile diſpoſition happen violat peruert lawes ſo neceſſarie auncient inſtitution nature vertue ſubiect ſelfe yet oughte bee touched wyth cauſe ſuche faulte deſerue noted corruption ſeinge ſuche derogation procedes abuſe hym knoweth perfection thynge falles alſo experience diuerſe accidentes beinge vertues ſelues loaſe theyr credit malice ſuche abuſe vyllanouſlye whervpon good thynge often condemned folly ſuche ignoraunt perfection ſame appeares rare diſpoſition bountifull mind ſo farre abhominable ſpot ingratitude lyfe ready bee offred ſatiſfaction diſcharge curteſie required wherein maye ſee greate effectes true magnanymitye wherein noble mynde oughte bee ouercome vertue honeſte curteſye ſo touchynge price victorye meane whiche three moſte meritorious commendacion deſerueth weare garland referre iudgement thindifferencie ſuche wythout paſſion parcialitye doe vſe note chaunces happenynge men ſee mortall enemye ſorowed miſerie aduerſarie ſolycited thereunto ſaye ineuitable force loue whiche alſo wroughte delyuerye marched wyth glorye preſent ſo rare greateſt monarcke worlde maye aſtonyed remembraunce prodigall bountie wonderfull zeale affection ſyſter towardes brother chalengeth leſſe praiſe reſte albeyt ſhe ſéene proof curteſye enemye yet ſhe aſſurance modeſtie notwythſtandynge diſcharge euerye waye dutye towardes brother ſhe layde virginitye vppon blocke vyolacion fyrſte claymeth bee victor becauſe laſte vertue mariage excedes former curteſie hath ouerthrowen enemie feelde ſo enioye prayſe price victorye abſolute reſolution younge ladye kyll herſelfe ſhe forced diſhonnour againſte wyll take awaye glorie commendacion yf care kepe honour virginitye dyd preuaile aboue preſeruation lyfe brother thirde crew albeyt prodigal offer proceded compulcion former bountye hys frende yet noblenes hys mynde equall reſte hys vertue nothynge inferiour eyther twoo yet yf ſinguler reſpecte retourne hys benefytt wyth double intereſt wyth care bee ſufficientlye thankefull patrone coulde dyminiſhe hys glorye wherein becauſe lamentable tragedye twoo poore louers ſōmones diſcouer theyr miſaduenture wyth leſſe reaſon furniſhe ſtage declaracion theyr loyaltye ladyſhip hath alredye harde whole diſcourſe rare vertues syenna leaue ſuche gentleman ſkilful dame take paine ſkan hiſtorye argue cauſe large reſolue iudgement leaſure doubtynge integritye yeldynge true tytle tryumphe glorie ſome one three whome accompte moſte worthie bee crowned lawrel victorye finis argument nothinge good profytable ſo euer appeare whereon attendethe diſcommodytie hym deales wythout diſcrecion together perentorye diſpleaſure receiuing contrarye conſent good gouernemēt wherin may aſſiſted ſufficient confirmation daylye experience ordynarye meates brothes confeccions tollerated phizicke ſuſtentacion man whiche albeit bee good theim ſelues yet ſwallowed glottonous ſort procure ſurfeyt vnſauery indiſgeſtion alſo conuerting aunciente healthe force nature humor debylytie deſtillinge thorowe partes bodye corrupte blodde ſelfe afore pure without infection euen ſuche diſpoſition loue whoſe effectes directed reaſon whiche oughte guide euerie accion man ſuche enemy deede quiet lyfe neceſſary meanes reforme rudenes owne nature accordinge authorytie poet affirminge loue rudeman reduced cyuilitie foole learneth wiſedom cowarde becomes valiaunte couetouſe nigard sondry vertues loue ſettes purſe wyde open hys frende neyther kinde curteſye wherwith hee loue doth participat make experience contrarye meane without aduiſe iudgemente throwe himſelfe hedlonge golphe foliſhe ronning phantaſye eſcapes hardly without rewarde whiche frantike paſſion yeldeth ordenarely ſuche vnhappelye partaker ſuche infection neyther thinge furthereth ruyne dekaie man ſuffriuge eye vnderſtandinge ſeeled ſuche ymitate ymate glott gredy deſyers whiche nature hathe enioyned eſtates honour embrace ſpeciall vertue trulye thinkes foliſhe infortunat crewe mighte reſerue therrours deſtructions others ſpeciall pattornes preceptes reſtraine humor owne madnes whiche aware ledd brinke mortall deſtruction albeit thindiſcretion miſerable ſorte ſeames nothinge vnlike comparaiſon thoſe hauinge longe vſed trade thefte robberye ſeinge companion paſſe ſentence corde lacke grace notwithſtandinge diſclaime wickednes wherin haue bene nozeled ſo many yeares neyther plage rather iuſte puniſhmente thinge inferior makinge chiefe glorye whiche moſte imperfecte loue eyther ſo ſubiecte diſpaire beaſtely aſſotted withe greedye encownter pleaſure fynde procuring theyr owne folly want order proceſſe fatall ſommaunce entrey felycitye forced reſigne one inſtante lyfe loathinge contentmente leſſe contynuance paine loue ſeame greuous mynde hath ye gift paſſe theim ouer reaſon like vehement inwarde greffe mynd proceding wardesyou hope lawe nature loue ſyſter wardes brother excuſe diligence indeuor vſe preſerue life holde leſſe deare tendreſt part myne eye wherwith camilla without argumentes ſome litle femynine anger argumente mortall perill perſon afore demaunded heare aunſwere vnmarked ye girle ſhe preuented thoffer daunger contrary camilla tolde feare inconuenience hys ſoddayne traunce declared vnto albeit miſtres ſo quick conſet hisextremitie required yet hart ſo hard frozen meanes thawe neyther aunſwere without hope although firſte ſhee ſeamed obiecte diſloyalety ordenarye ficcyon men willinge hym reſt abandon diſpaire arminge ſelfe corage dyſmiſſe ſolytarie ſauage order lyfe wherin increaſe vncerteyne conſolation ſhe tolde albeit yet foxemone reaſon aduaunce hym ſelfe ſo farre craue mutuall conferrence yet nede forbeare write wyth conſent tyme place ſhe woulde deliuer letter wyth inde uor bringe laſt reſolution wher albeit ſhee ſeamed feede tyme wyth intente make hym diſcontynue fancy attempting notwithſtandinge wonderfull ympoſſibilitie hee ſo ſtalled amarus golphe al pilottes belonginge infynit galies venice lackt force hale hym yet ſeamed ſhe thereby breathe ayre freſhe comforte partes languiſhinge brother likinge aduiſe determyned put councell execution whervppon one ſuperficiall ſkil writinge thytalyan verſe compoſed certeine elegie conteynynge ſome ſorowe ſubſtance requeſt ſayeth offence preferr good madam excuſe lord maiſter vpon whoſe behalfe craued ſo muche fauour reade letter kiſſed wit great humilitye offred chaſte mayde knowyng meſſenger ſhe ſéen hym often follow traine gonſaldo gaue iudgement alſo cauſe commynge wherefore ſhe refuſe alſo wyth certeine tearmes reproche retourned hym anſwer cōtrarie thexſpectation hym ſelfe contentment hym ſent hym ſayeth ſhe doth maiſter accompte ſuch ſimplicitie haue longe ſince diſcerned thintēt follie doth thinke one ſettes deare price mine honor beſt ladie italy opiniō reſpect authoritie greatnes degrée force ye alſo enterlarde ymportunities wyth doble vehemencye go moſt buſilye abowte make praie bewtie fragilitie whereof albeit accompt onlye one nomber alſo leſſe deſloyall reſt yet reſpectinge reputacion race content geue credit wordes accept offer ſuch ſort haue promiſed reappoſing ſo muche ſelfe youre diſcrecion ſhall appere want thing belongeth gouernmēt wiſe conueigh ſuch ſecret affaire wherin fid effect exſpectaciō ſelf ſhal iudge liberalitie retorning merite honeſt frendſhipp wherwyth thalteracion breache countenance face argued preſent troble contrarietie mynde whiche therle conſtruinge procede deſyer ſhe moue hym diſmiſſe delay diſpoſe hymſelfe thexecution thinge ſo indiffrentlie deſyered theym bothe put diligence thankefull offer tyme fortune ſuch ſorte embraſinge wyth thowſande furniſhed freſhe ſupplie ſo part founde ſo delicate behalfe reſigned thoritie whiche earſte gouerned hym doinges order derection ſuche ſort ſpake nothing mouthe blanche marya thing wherin councell ſpedie meane recouer thobiect deſier ſhe ſeamed enter tormentes diſpair alſo make ſmal accompte vſe longer lyfe iudging thexterior outewarde promiſes younge lorde ſeamed ſufficient quenche thurſte ij earneſt ſolicitours loue reuenge one ſewinge conſommacion wicked deuiſe prickyng deſier procure theffect newe affection wyth ſeconde earle albeyt ſhe diſplayed ſuche manyfeſte ſygnes good wyll eyther arte loue coulde imagyne wanton idle brayne deuiſe yet ſeynge ſo ſlender replye parte withe encreaſe burning appetite ſhe thought neceſſarie put ſpurs dull diſpoſicion makinge conſcience become requeſte ſuche generall awe ouer eſtates peculiar authoritie puniſhe v woman vehemencye affection deſyeringe thinges whiche nature hath forbidden v attempte onelye diſpenſe raſhe follye diſpoſe ſelfe take awaye leaſte diminiſh greatnes preſent paſſion whiche founded fyrſt vppon generall fame vertues ſo often viewe rare perfection perſon ſince repaire pauya hath forced ſuche increaſe zeale aggrauacion deſyer deſtenie denye ſpedye ſupplye reléefe fortune forbide come viſitt longyng eſtate crueltye ſhall mortifye paſſion giue ende lyfe together wherein ſeinge loue hath fauored wyth victorie conqueſte earſte power vanquiſhe men ſhowe ſelfe leſſe willynge embrace benefytt worthie glorye deferr ſyr expoſe effectes pitie behalfe lyueth onely vnder mercie ſimple hope whiche yf retourne reſolucion make fruſtrate conuerte deſyer ayre ſame ſhall alſo pronounce fatall ende vnhappie moſte loyall blanche maria embaſſage commiſſion mouth bringer ſturred vp ſmal alteracion mynde younge earle chieflye ſawe hymſelfe purſued franke offer whiche yf affectioned zeale bare deare frende companion lorde valpergo ſtayed thattempte ſoughts longe ſince obteine albeit iudged neyther tollerable humanitie thoffice gentleman ſupplant pleaſure frende marche ſteppes praye yet charmed vehement wordes letter opinion diſcurteſie greate abuſe liberal offer ſo faire ladye gaue place ſommonce wente immediatlye houſe fyndynge voyede companie bedd chamber ſawe ſmall occaſion preferr halfe circumſtance courtlike wooing wiche seigneur valpergo vſed one certeine intiſinge kiſſes monethes ſuch ſorte therle ſo aſſotted became ſo ydolatrous behalfe performed deuocion ſaint ſauing vnſeamely ſhryne new mynion alſo ſeing ſtāde water chin whollie ſubiect yoke awe determined kepe harde hande bridle intent make hym bloddye executioner deteſtable deuiſe againſt former louer valpergo whoſe felicitie defended eyther frō peril imaginacion el god wold yet gyue leaue wickednes hope deceiued touching help aſſiſtance newe frend valpergo ſeing himſelf onely diſpoſſeſſed loue ladye diſhonored mouthe wyth diuerſe wordes reproche hys abſence iudged grudge conſcience myniſter ſemblable tearmes rage fyndynge greate difficultie dyſgeſte thyngratitude loſte louer whoſe doynges notwithſtandynge ſhée allowed ſome tymes iuſtice ſawe ſome reaſon hys reuenge inorderlie dealynge opened fyrſte way diſcurteſie flattered ſelfe vaine ymagynacion menne borne beare ympoſicions ſo euer ſuche tryflors ſhe woulde laye vppon theyme ſeynge ſeruantes dyd ryghte endure take good parte thynge ſayed theyr miſtres albeyt feedynge ſtill malicious coller certeine ſecret deſyer vengance determyned laſte retorne hys diſcourteſye leſſe intereſt loſſe hys lyfe reſolucion procure ſpedy effect hande hym ſhe preſumed haue ſo muche commaundement ſimple requeſte mouthe woulde make hym miniſter beholde ympudentie ragethys tygreſſe goth abowte arme one frende agaynſte yt coulde ſuffice abuſe ſelfe towardes theim bothe filthie vſe bodye intent morder one ſhe puttes hazarde equall deſtruction bothe confirmynge abhomynable adulterye wyth manſlaughter wyllfull morder ſynne moſte haynous affore god manne wherein morder moſt ha • nous ſighte god fretting mynde colde admitt neyther quiett contentemēt til eye wer witneſſes theffect deuiſe leaſte ſhe put intent vpon tearmes hym ſhe ment make bloddie boocher beaſtely wyll ſo attendynge offer conuenient tyme place ſhe aſſiſted laſt ſo farfurth one nyght bedd together chiefeſt delite theyr pleaſant excerciſe ſhe burſte ſoddainly vehement teares ſighes ſignes dollour ſuche ſorte wyth counterfaite alarams whiche inwarde ſorowe ſeamed miniſter ſet broache paſſion appeared ſo mortall ignoraunt bedfelowe thinkynge ſoule bodye point make preſent ſeperacion one enquired cauſe grefe wyth addicion yt yt came diſpleaſure wronge man handes onely ſhould gyue reuenge wyth abſolute contentement ſelfe hereafter wherewyth vſing aduauntage promiſe wherein ſhe accompted ſufficiencie procure ende enemye tolde hym entreateth ſecond frend kyll firſte louer nature gyuen certeine facilitie vile baſe ſorte people beare brooke offer iniurie ſo nothynge contrarye condicion noble mynde bee touched wyth ſuch villanie puttes honor intereſt renowme vppon tearmes publike infamie ſaye thuſmuche ſyr ſayth ſhe wéeting face wyth dewe waterie eye venemous basila loued without meaſure abſteine violacion thinnocent blood frende whome lawe frendſhypp forbad hym waye abuſe albeit appeaſe preſent rage counteſſe promiſed effect deſyer wyth ſpedye wiſdom woulde ſuffer hym ſturre vp ſyniſter reporte without great occaſion part beſides conſidered iuſtice quarell reſted hym taken pray yt mouth albeit procurement diſcontinued hawnte courſe repayre thether eraminyng circunſtance large founde cauſe farre inſufficient moue breache frendſhipp betwene theim determinynge continue league contented wyth diſſembled promiſe reſtored meane tyme exerciſe omitted neyther occaſion expedicion often came houſe ſhe eyther ſicke troubled wyth bulynes ſhe coulde kepe hym companie lettynge ſomtime ſhoott gate againſt diſcontinueth frēdſhip vvith lord gaiazo hym whiche becauſe ſhe ſawe lacked force make hym refraine ſhe retired thaſſiſtance pollecie deſyeryng hym wyth ſimple colde termes ſo muche honor forbeare henſfurth acceſſ houſe ſhe mynde retourne diſſembled teares féele remorce conſcience behalfe longe abuſe haue vſed towardes hym albeit offence faultes may excuſed pardoned procedynge follye ſeames altogether worthye frée pardon yet maye appeare ſome ſorte excuſable ſo confeſſeth faulte gyueth greate argument amendement reſtoreth treſpaſſe ſufficient recompenſe deſyerynge ende haue leſſe conſideracion preſent caſe heretofore haue attempte recouerie firſte louer valpergo wherin notwithſtandinge apeared equalitie doubt difficultie chieflie ſhe feared laſte left diciphered intent wyth reuelacion meane ſhe deuiſed procure hys deathe enterpriſe dare attempte whoſe mynde bondeman ſlaue ſyn wherin albeit beginninge ſeame ymport certeine difficultie ſoule preferreth reſiſtance conſcience waueringe moued remorſe remembrance shame neceſſarie age avve yong mē age deueſted honeſte ſhame perill make one affraied ymputacion reproch geue cauſe bluſhe like ympudent pyemount •• ſe renewinge traffique aunciente wickednes practiſed ſo far wyth familiar frendes hym whoſe deathe harde ſhe earſte conſpired malice excuſinge herſelfe ſo amplie embaſſages letter vehement perſwacion content heare ſort ſhe hable purge ſelfe article regiſtred ſeales put night folowinge lorde valpergo reſtored poſſeſſion fortreſſe whiche earſte reuolted lyued longe dnder awe prince wherin thus renewed rounde amarous daunce one fynding ſkoape libertie vnder recouered louer afore reſolued whollie obſerue thappetite ladie beholde ſeconde deſyer blodd ſuggeſtion morder appearing eftſones face megera croppinge altogether hearbe reuenge bloddie enterpriſes ſhee accompted pryncipall vertue commit miſchieues greateſte deteſtacion whyche notwythſtandynge rewarde mordore thondered vppon death due revv •• de morder laſte wyth ſhamefull miſerable ende ſelfe vntymelye deathe hym fyrſt companion next neighbour follie wyth equall perticipacion filthie pleaſure reappoſed muche truſte villenie preferred vice afore vertue toke pleaſure deuiſe bloddie affaire whereof ſhall haue diſcourſe large laſt act hiſtorie blanche marya ſeinge ſo rempierd harte valpergo worde currant commaunde hym determyned prefer hym thoffice morderer vppon perſon hym earſt refuced charge wherin addinge expedicion deuiſe one night beinge bedd together ſhe embraſed feaſted frankly wyth filthie folly loue wherein ſhe ſufficient experience ſhee diſcontynued kiſſes wyth ſoddaine ſcilence drawinge traiſon farr tolde hym longe ſince ſhe preſent hym wyth one requeſt ſpeciall fauour wherin becauſe ſhee doubted eyther moue hys diſpleaſure receiue repulſe ſhe hathe onely defferred ymportunate ſtayed declare cauſe whyche ſayth ſhe althoughe touche leſſe ſauegarde lyfe vnworthie infamye deare blanche marya yet reſpecte fauor ſuch authoritie wyth rather vſe ſcilence frendſhipp contentment bee thawthor thinge ſhould incenſe anger gaue libertie make demaund aſſurance hys part performe effect price ſo euer ſaith matter ymport perill behoueth vſe care lyfe honor abuſed ſelfe deſtreſſed ymagyne diligence put reuenge wronge vndertake quarelles wherfore doubte good ladye ymploye hym lyuethe ſerue readye dye doo pleaſure ſhee aſked hym frendeſhyype betwene therle gaiazo hym aſſuraunce hee hadde hys loyaltie ſuche experience ſaythe hee nothinge hable diſſolue amytie woulde ſtande intreated offer bodie preſente daunger remoue hys perill hee ſewer woulde make anye conſcience redéeme extremetie wyth hazarde hys owne lyfe neyther doo wée vſe thenne common conuerſacion thinges betwene v nowe cauſe youre queſtion wherewyth traitreſſe ſeynge ſufficiente wordes paſſed circumſtance thought e nowe tyme broach vente poyſon wherefore kiſſynge hym amarous ſorte thenne euer hée felte hym ſelfe embraſed afore tolde hym poynies wherein hée deceiued touchynge truſte hee ſeamed reappoſe hys frende ſaythe ſhée ſoo conſtante aſſured hys behalfe hee full villanyein dyſſemblynge thée malice whyche hee hathe longe hatched vnder winge hys deceytful harte vſe ſimple playnes ſoo ſewer caſe haue cauſe geue uone iudgemente hym thenne youre moſte cruell capitall ennemye worlde wherein becauſe wyll preſſe credulous dreame moue beleue anye thynge whoſe author ſufficiente authoritie yon ſhal vnderſtande hee aduowched noo leſſe thenne haue reapported breathe hys owne mouthe ſuche tyme hee practyſed wyth mee youre late abſence wyth thys addycion hee ſhoulde neuer enioy perfectte quiett mynd taſte benefite aſſured reſte reappoſe til hand made morſells body deuyded al partes ſmall peces confirmynge ſame inſtaunte hys bloddye reſolucion othe honoure lyfe gentlemanne wythin compaſſe noo longe tyme hee woulde bydde ſuche banquette ſhoulde neede anye longer bee carefull worlde myndefull make loue ladyes wherein hee ſeamed ſo reſolute groūded malice notwithſtandyng perſuacions colde prefer colde neuer wreſt originall cauſe mortall grudge albeit tyme entred termes collour agaynſte iuſtice ſpite reaſon preuent perill ſhowe fauor ſauynge life yet remembrance auncient loue vertue halfe mortefied dead moued ſuche remorſe behalfe dyd onlye thuttermoſt indeuor remoue vaile entent alſo deſyered hym teares deſyſte ſuche enterpriſe whileſt place abode cold endure viewe iniury much leſſe ſee diſtreſſed death ſpedie ſacrafyce myne owne lyfe whereunto gaue onely deaff eare bounde efteſones former proteſtacion ſeconde othe eyther hys dead carkaſſe place ſhold witnes hys good wil el wolde delyuer world lord valpergo meane thē imparte vnto reaſon abſence ſmall acceſſe hether wherein ſir ſeing ſince thē felicitie hath defended daunger conſomacion intent ſo nowe beſeche ſtande vppon garde defending malice alſo preuent pernicius reſolucion acte equall curteſye yt wyſdome take awaye lyfe enemie giuinge place malice comit bodye mercie morderinge hande beſides yt breache vertue requite thintent iniurie effect equall reuēge wiſdom ſhold greater eſtimacion traiſon haynous hathe firſt abuſed broken lawe frendſhyp dreſſinge ſuche mortall ambuſhes againſte ſo deare frende wherein part haue diſcouered whole conſpiracie vnder franke reapport vnfained trueth ſo beinge leſſe carefull ſauetie curius myne owne lyfe waghinge theim ballance indifferent zeale wiſhe followe aduiſe preuentyng ſo ymmynent daunger aſſurance ſauetie offer thaſſalte hym hathe alreadye ſworne deſtruction wherein alſo ſhall performe vertue valyant knyghte full ſatiſfaction deſyer nott ſo amplie gratefye preſented fre gifte beſt dukedome italye nowe ſhall ſee effect loue beare efteſones deſiereth ſuffer liue longer triumpheth without meaſure vnworthie ſlaunder moſt affectionate blanche maria yf laſte wordes foliſhe lady broughte whole requeſte ſuſpicion importunity peraduenture procured conſent therle conferrynge pointes diſcourſe vehemencie perſuading founde deede chiefeſt meanyng tended defence owne quarell wherevppon entred pawſe meaſuring ſecret mynde tearmes preſent malice thexperience diuerſe proffes fydelitie frende knewe aſſured vertue thē ymagyn ſo great villanie againſt albeit knewe yt fetche lady ſowe ye ſeedes quarrel betwene therle gaiazo yet flatter fond humor ye time promiſſed become myniſter curſed wherewyth ended diſcourſe betwene ij young lord euer forgatte contynue remembraunce theyr venemous basilike wyth woordes oppen infamye companye ſo euer bothe intiſynge meanes ſhe hadde traine menne neyther bluſhed ſame moued remorſe wyth viewe euill diſgeſted one wyth ordynarie face ſhameles complexion wherein notwithſtanding ſhe neyther ſo preciſe conſtant inwarde grypes ſhe felt almoſte forced myneordynar ie ſo amongeſt reſt repayre acceſſe houſe vyſited wyth often hawnt two earles equall nobylytie ſemblable diſcent honor albeit vſed indifferente countenaunce expoſing great argument famylyaritie behalfes ſe ſhow euery gentlemā yet forgetting theſtymacion owne race ranke hold haue ſemed late ſo vnthankfull honor vſed towards fynd returne meryt curteſye wyth general brute open vnder coollor deuacion communicate matter bawdry ſo part let kepe hath pay hym ſelfe ye tribut folly reſolued hēſfurth ſpeke hym alſo ſhonne place wher venemous ſerpent rauenous wolfe rather head yt although ſhe wer excellēt ye gyfts oratour belōged one trade yet durſte ſhe neyther truſte ſmoth ſugred ſtile tounge excuſinge cauſe comming ſeme efteſones credite fynes wytt deuiſyng newe youth peſtilence worſe infectiō ſayng beſides yt yt ſent gaue ſufficiēt profe follie ſeking ſeduce money preſents yt toke pittie teares former complaint dolor neyther leſſe vyle thincke buye money y laſt threates ſtroke ſuch feare hart olde hag preſent diſpaier preuaile waie purſute queſt glad eſcape ſo wel danger deferuing ſhe retired haſt ſeely ferraroys whome place good newes pleſant reporte ſucceſſe ſhe myniſtred perſwacions correct hys fancye forgett loue ſuche one make accompte hys ſeruice willing withal plant hys affection ſome better ſoyle vpon ſuche one brutiſhe voyd reaſon requyt meryt ſeruice ſaieth ſhe thies beaſts impes whithout wit order ciuilitie alſo lack diſcreſion conſider caſes loue yelde due méede true affection neither degenerat climat baſe diſcent thinge ſuche wilfull loare follie doth lead vnto beyng fauored nature gyfte certen beautie whiche bringes eſtimacion amongeſt men ſo aſſotted humor ſelfe ſeme rather abuſe benefyte ſo precious iewel worthie weare ſo rare ornament ſayeth ſhe moued prayer preſent anye deuiſe ſerue reclaime haggard mynd ſeaming quarrel wyth offer curteſie cannot thyncke y ſome hard rocke conuerted ſhappe woman fygure beautie recouery ceaſe longer féede humor paſſion remembrance ſemes take pleaſure youre gryef well well ſayth dolorous louer woulde coulde eaſely forget apte perſwad thuſmuch aduiſed afore gaue aſſuraunce communicate wyth ſelleth youre aduiſe money make youre trauayle marchaunt fylthye gaine albeyt ſeynge want diſcreſion hath ſtyrred vp error folly youth preuayled aboue force wiſdom muſte dryuen make neceſſytye lawe geue place ye ſentēce preſēt fortune greuing withſtā dynge frendſhyppe vndouted zeale affection bare ſhold reape fruts rigour receue meryite vertue handes crueltie leaſt wil ſo diſpair argument future hope ſhall kepe breathe expectyng benefytt better time wil comitt ſelfe gouerment pacience haue harde onely tuche ſtone trye man y fallen termes affliction galland ſemed rather féede tyme bynd himſelfe performe theffecte owne wordes neyther mente ſuffer hys laſt reſolution paſſe currant money muche leſſe content hym ſelfe cardes ſeyng lyked game ſeing colde preuaile pollicye wyn fort ſomonce offer compoſicion determined laſte helpe vſe vttermoſte hys force performe hys conqueſt ſo euer yt coſt thuſmuch waye ther y nogreate enterprice ende ſo euer tende whether yt bée guided vertue conducted vice whoſe effecte aunſwere therpectacion thinuentour onleſſe ther roumthe reſerued thirde perticipate therein aſwel erpedicion cauſe ſuer conueyghe myſterye ſoo thys vallet chamber reſolued abſolutely purſuete hys queſte imparteth diſcourſe hys loue paſſed hys ſynyſter ſucceſſe ſame hys dyuerſe aſſalttes forte hys fundrie ſharpe repulſes daſhbuckler buſhops made conſcience bee miniſter euil ye outlawes ſhooters hil vſe curteſie ſtripping marchauntes ſend london penyles budgettes forgate alſo make preuye hys laſte reſolucion crauyng therein aſſyſtaunce hys fryndeſhyppe ſuche ſorte vppon thynſtant made hym aduowe ſame thuttermoſte power onelye ſayeth deuiſe waye diligence ſhall declare zeale bere thee deſire haue place thée boſome thy felicitie yt follie ſaieth deſperat louer reiterate order former deuiſes preſent efteſones office curteſie time loſt onlie reſtes offer racke meane oppreſſe force neyther doo care peny worth made life ſo may ſort reuenge obſtinate crueltie peraduenture firſt taſte pleſant iewyſtes loue wil ſlacke bridle rigour conuert harde angrye clymate inuincible humor diſpoſicion leſſe difficultie ſhe eaſier hereafter intreated neither wold beginning euery thing ſeames harde haue reſpect dāger impoſſibilitie thē terprice conſidering beginninge al thinges importe certeine difficultie oncet geuen worſte paſte cauſe feare doubt remaynes waighinge pleſure thou ſhalt ymagine alſo depely thou ſhalt leue thie debte wil ſtody requite yt wyth lyke haue el may ſtande ſteade wherwyth preuailed ſo muche ouer vyperous inclynacion hys cotreatur albeit knew hys conſent weare ſo wicked ye ye acte deteſtable yet waighīg ye preſet offer frendſhip wt great authoritie wt byſſhoppe forgetinge duetie hys conſcience confirmed eftſones conſent willinge deſolate louer take harte graſſe repoſe himſelfe chiefely vpon aide hys frendſhippe becauſe ſayth chiefe conveighe thys myſterie conſiſtes conſente conuenyente tyme place let youer whole indeuour watche whenne ſhee goeth fieldes alone thend vſinge aduantage may haue time oure feate wythout dread danger ſo ſoone agreed vpon betwene two theffect folowed expedicion momente craftie louer marked diligently howers tymes ordynary labor neither cold ſhe haunt ſo ſecret place eye redye diſcouer ſo lyeng ambuſhe way vſuall trade corne feldes laſt brought ſtale imparted marrow ſailed followe trace ſofte ſubtil manner wilie coms ſpoile powltrye fermor ſo circumſpecte doinge leaſt noyſe worlde make hym take bu • til hys feare bee paſſed thys ferrrarois fellowe purſewed pore maide ſuch ſecret vnknowen wayes wyth ſpede thenne neceſſarie thexecucion good lawful buſines clyente appered backe afore ſhee ware hauinge time ſpende circumſtaunce ſaluted wyth cauſe hys commynge thys ſort lengthe tyme true tuch ſtone try difference betwene fained harte firme affeccion haue ſufficient proofe conſtancy long ſeruice wyth ſincere loyaltie may ſeme meritorious alone iudge diligence accuſe crueltie trybute true frendſtippe paide wyth replie ſemblable affection doo thys ſort ſuſpende ſute doblinge paſſion denying thynge due iuſt title thus longe kepe captiuitie offer lyfe ranſome ſue right reward wyth crueltie haue deſerued leſſe ſeminge one calibre calling time nowe ſtrike ſaile remoue vaile ancyente rigor whereof haue taſted long time waighynge indifferently meryt martirdom yelde meede accordingly let taſte vertue bownty aſwell haue hetherto lyued vnder yoke youre crueltye ſo méede owne deſer uing may laſt geue end euils whych ſuffer meanes wherwyth poore iulya leſſe amaſed ſodein encownter place vnprouided anſwere doubtefull demaunde dryuen replie according ſhortnes tyme leaſure appeale length tyme declaracion loyal loue proffe conſtancy ſayth ſhe craue iudge fowle deſier rather robb holde moſte dere honor offer true affeccion wherin iuſtified diuerſe diſorderly meanes whych heretofore haue ſuborned aduaunce wicked intent neyther deſerue right thimputacion crueltie much leſſe vnſemely rigor terme conſidering neither vſed one ſpecial vertue defence myne honeſtie touching paſſion tormēt procedyng rather want diſcrecion ſelf occaſion onmy part ſee neither cauſe complayne grefe reaſō releue neither anſwe termes commit themeryt follye wiſhinge geue end euilis preſſe power ſeinge neither preſſe beginning cauſe ye continuance much leſſe experienced cure ſuch diſcaſes pray forbere eftſones purſewe beinge equall haue ſaide qualytie callinge leſſe redy agre wyth conſent fulfill beaſtely appetyte deſiringe ende let lyue ſerue henſforth wyth proceſſe vaine ym portunyties hadde rather indure martirdome thouſand torment thinge myne honor iuſtifie wher regarding good eye ye fierce countenance enemy arguing ye preſent troble minde fearing withal ſecret inſtinct hart nere approche euil torne began amend pace alſo ſhe dobled one yt durſt • ſhe moſt abhorred loth loſe benefyte ſo good time leſſe willing haue ſo ſwete morſel takē mouth fained certein offer ſeruice conduct ye towne preferring therwt freſhe diuerſe requeſtes take pittie paſſion albeit ſhe hard wythout aunſwere yet power paſſe hand deſtinie tyme brought place conuenient thexecution hys execrable enterpriſe far frō town ye ordenary hawnt company beſt fauored intent myddeſt corne fielde couert moſt conuenient ſuch act wher hauing one part play taketh offer kiſſe albeit ſhe reſiſted vttermoſt litle ſtrength cryeng againſte force fowle meaning yet time loſt conſidering ſhe ymedyatly aſſailed perſwading ſcilence ſaid brauery great one calling came thither myniſters infection ſaing although villeny force hath defiled chaſtitie body geuen theffecte laſciuious deſier yet ſhold neuer hable eyther wyth money wayes corrupt ſincerytie hart whoſe innocencye ſaith ſhe wyl tryumphe ouer thy execrable acte afore yelde due hyer thy trauaile thy power ſatiſfie leue cōtented yt frō al yt world cānot eftſones reſtore god whō muſt claime ſatiſfactiō ivlia void companie ſauyng doleful ecchoes woodes ryuers anſwered cryes wyth lyke complaint renewes warre preſent deſaſter tearing heares without reſpecte quarellyng ye dowery nature gyuen wold gladly herſelfe order go houſe father euill • ucke home ſhe put beſte garment ſhe attyring ſelf order go ſome great méeting banquet ſhittes doare cotage leading yonger ſyſter hād went furthwith awnt one alaram ſorowes ſhe fel ſodeinly qualme paſſion ſoundyng wherein ſhe remayned traunced wythout argument lyfe til helpe aſſiſtāce ſhe eftſones delyuered thuſe libertie ſenſes quarelling ſtil wt horror fact deſire reuenged death ſhe ſeamed rebuke owne ymbecillitie faintnes corage ſaing ſigne vertu ſeame ſhrink argumēts conſtancy ought chiefly tappere wyll deſire lyue hath loſt renoume honor ought parte loth alredy remembrance lyfe ſeing haue loſt chefeſt pillor ſame wherof meane make ſpedy declaracion ſentence haue alredy pronounced ende wherin ſhall appeare worlde although bodye haue taſted wherfore pray ſuffer thaſſurance vertue worke force correctinge ronning appetit follie wyll make mayſter ſelfe let ſo vaine thinge ſimple glaunce bewtie apte declyne hable indure preuaile aboue aunciente eſtimacion honor draw wythout lymittes bondes callinge parte haue incloſed myne honor life together one veſſell wyth intent make preſente theym bothe one inſtant hym beſeche maye god take awaye traunce reſtore entyer defende mée tymes thinuaſion ſo pernicious enemye ſayth wythout ſome argument collor ſeame altogether vnworthy fauor likely performe thoffer ſeruice one quod ianiqneta oughte wyll paſſe graunt good wyll ſuche lawe churche conſente frendes ſhall enioyne marie neither agreater wrong eſtimacion embaſing greatnes becom ſeruant ſo pore mayde albeit contented make equallitie indifferent diſtribucion greatnes eſtate wyth litle eſtymacion tune hath preferred vnto yet grudge cōſcience quarrelling foulnes ye act wil neither ſuffer admit offer conſēt requeſt deſiring end exchang intent make preſent ſeruice ſome knoweeth requit ſo great courteſie better neyther like phraſe circunſtance muche leſſe determyn ſpende lōger tyme wherewith albeit began harde condicion thy preſente bavvde vvoeth ianiquette ſtate fynde ſame ſubiecte clymatt longe contynuance hope apte reliued induſtrie thy parent albeit haue retofore enioyed goodnes fortune borne porte honeſte callynge rich yet thowe ſeeſte nowe daunger deſolatiō fallen ſo farre mallice pouertie wante meanes ſupplie needy diſpoſicion owne lyfe alſo preferr aduauncemente due thy deſeruyng greue leſſe alſo ſee flower thy youth ſlyp away ſuch ſtealthe pyninge miſery thy parēts impedimēt prefermēt thy beauty albeit honored nōber wt offer marriage yet whē thei haue ſifted thy ſtate olde neighbour leſſe exſpectacion heare whyche ſhe ymagyned leaſt enquired opynion aduiſe ſaith ſhée knowe driue ſome amaſe firſte thinge neyther conuenient myne age ſeamely callynge diſagreing wholly ianeqvetta one paragon honeſtie age noriſhe reſpect vertue thonlye cauſe admiracion procuringe chieflye recourſe bable people rather cuſtome creditt deſier companye reſt ſayth bable people rather longe importunityes luchyn greate preſentes proffer promiſſes large price coulde ſtirre remoue ſeate conſtancie feles nowe ſuche alteracion fortune ſhe pointe ſurrender ſelfe whiche neyther power become maiſter worde aduouche pointes late graunte pore gentleman ſuſpectynge one thoughte ſuche tyrannye miſtrys muche leſſe ſhoulde buye kiſſes ſo deare price tolde attended ſommonee cōmaundement vowe began euen enter pointes commaundement declarynge ſignes ſhe ſhould bée obeyed wherewith gaue humble reuerence retyred immediatly hys lodgynge faygnynge ſuche aboute hym extremetie colde rhume father lefte hym withoute awe authoritie albeit life father continuall hawnter berlea common diceſing houſe houſe vnthriftie exerciſes wante ſufficient demers furniſhe deſier ſkill caſting three deceitfull companion blacke white vppon ſquare table forced often tymes forbeare playe learne conynge lokyng vppon yet tyme owne diligence made hym ſo artificiall beyng cryer awme fewe hable excede ſleyghte caſtinge twelue affore ſixe two dyce tooke halfe ſo good accomte regarde courſe cardes yet notwithſtanding ſo wel grownded principle arte often tymes conyng beguilyng hym preuented contrarie ſleighte onelye purſe paide charge whole companye whiche vnmarked ſome two three famyliars hys father reſpect whoſe frendſhip vertue ſondrie argumentes ymynent deſtructiō ſonne moued theym enter
